const int PROP_FROZEN = 0;

// Player speed multiplier is 0,04375.

Actor PossessedPlasmaGunner : PossessedMonster
{
	Player.MorphWeapon "PlasmaGunnerWeapon"
	Player.ViewHeight 41
	Health 20
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 0.35 // FIXME: how to convert speeds?
	Mass 100
	PainChance 160
	+FLOORCLIP
	+MISSILEMORE
	SeeSound "fem/sight"
	PainSound "fem/pain"
	DeathSound "fem/death"
	ActiveSound "fem/active"
	Obituary "%o was melted by a Plasma zombie."
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		ZMAY A 10
		ZMAI A 10
		Loop
	See:
		ZMAY AABB 3
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		ZMAY CCDD 3
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		Loop
	Missile:
		ZMAY F 2 Bright
		ZMAY E 3
		ZMAY F 2 Bright
		ZMAY E 3
		ZMAY F 2 Bright
		ZMAY E 3
		ZMAY E 20
		ZMAY E 10
		Goto Spawn
	}
}

Actor PlasmaGunnerWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	States
	{
	Ready:
		PKPL A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		PLSF B 2 A_FireCustomMissile("ZombiePlasmaBall")
		PKPL A 3 Bright
		PLSF B 2 A_FireCustomMissile("ZombiePlasmaBall")
		PKPL A 3 Bright
		PLSF B 2 A_FireCustomMissile("ZombiePlasmaBall")
		PKPL A 3 Bright
		PKPL DEF 1
		PKPL G 7
		PKPL FED 2
		PKPL CBA 1
		Goto Ready
	Flash:
		TNT1 A 2 Bright A_Light1
		PLSF A 2 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		Stop
	}
}

Actor ZombiePlasmaBallMOP : ZombiePlasmaBall replaces ZombiePlasmaBall
{
	DamageType "Monster"
}


Actor PossessedRailGunner : PossessedMonster
{
	Player.MorphWeapon "RailGunnerWeapon"
	Player.ViewHeight 41
	Health 30
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 0.35
	Mass 100
	PainChance 140
	DropItem "HealthFlask" 55
	DropItem "ArmorCharge" 55
	DropItem "AmmoPack" 40
	DropItem "HandGrenadeAmmo" 100 1
	DropItem "MineAmmo" 50 1
	DropItem "NewCell" 100 20
	+FLOORCLIP
	+MISSILEMORE
	Obituary "%o caught a Railgunner's slug."
	SeeSound "grunt/sight"
	PainSound "grunt/pain"
	DeathSound "grunt/death"
	ActiveSound "grunt/active"
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		RPOS A 10
		RPOI A 10
		Loop
	See:
		RPOS AABB 3
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		RPOS CCDD 3
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
		Loop
	Missile:
		RPOS F 5 Bright
		RPOS E 40
		RPOS E 10
		Goto Spawn
	}
}

Actor RailGunnerWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	States
	{
	Ready:
		RAML ABC 2 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("railgunner/chargedshot")
		TNT1 A 0 A_FireCustomMissile("RailgunImpactRed")
		RAMF A 2 Bright A_RailAttack(Random(15,25), 0, 1, "Red", None, RGF_SILENT | RGF_NOPIERCING, 1, "MonsterNoPuff")
		RAMF B 3 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		RAMF CDEF 2
		RAMF GGG 1
		RAMF G 16
		Goto Ready
	}
}

Actor ShotgunZombieWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{

	States
	{
	Ready:
		SHTG A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(3,3,0,1,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,Random(6,-6))
		SHTF A 3 Bright A_FireBullets(22.5,0,3,Random(1,5)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
		SHTF B 2 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		SHTF CDEF 1
		SHTG BCDEFG 1
		SHTG G 2 A_PlaySound("weapons/12gsgcock")
		SHTG HI 2
		SHTG J 1 A_SpawnItemEx("ShellCasing",30,-2,25,Random(2,4),Random(3,6),Random(3,6),0)
		SHTG IHGF 1
		SHTG EDCB 1
		Goto Ready
	}
}

Actor SuperShotgunZombieWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	States
	{
	Ready:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken", 2, "Ready2")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken", 1, "Ready1")
		Goto Ready0
	Ready2:
		SHTE A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Ready1:
		SST2 A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Ready0:
		SHT2 A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Loop
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken",1,"AltFire")
	FireBoth:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/sshotf")
		TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(6,3,0,1,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SSGZombieToken",2)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAA 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,Random(6,-6))
		SH2F A 2 Bright A_FireBullets(13.8, 9.6, 10, Random(1,4)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
		SH2F B 2 Bright A_Light2
		SH2E A 1 A_Light0
		SHT2 B 1
		SHT2 CDEF 1
		SHT2 EDCB 2
		Goto ReloadBothInstant
	AltFire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken",2,"Reload")
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/ssgsingleshot")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
		TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(3,3,0,1,0)
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,Random(6,-6))
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken",1,"FireLeft")
	FireRight:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SSGZombieToken",1)
		S2SF A 2 Bright A_FireBullets(22.5,0,3,Random(1,5)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
		S2SF B 2 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		SH2R ABCD 1
		SST2 A 4
		Goto Ready
	FireLeft:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("SSGZombieToken",1)
		S2SF C 2 Bright A_FireBullets(22.5,0,3,Random(1,5)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
		S2SF D 2 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		SH2R EFGH 1
		SHTE A 4
		Goto Reload
	Reload:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken",2,"ReloadBoth")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SSGZombieToken",1,"ReloadLeft")
		Goto Ready
	ReloadBoth:
		SHT2 RQ 2
	ReloadBothInstant:
		SH2E B 2
		SHT2 GH 2
		SH2E F 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/sawedopen")
		SHT2 I 1
		SH2E G 1
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SSGShellCasing",25,-2,25,Random(2,4),Random(-3,-6),Random(3,6),0)
		SH2E D 4
		SHT2 J 2
		SH2E EH 2
		SHT2 K 3
		SHT2 L 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/shellslide")
		TNT1 A 0
		SHT2 M 2
		SHT2 N 2
		SHT2 OP 1
		SH2E I 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/sawedclose")
		SH2E C 1
		SH2E B 2
		SHT2 QR 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("SSGZombieToken", 2)
		Goto Ready
	ReloadRight:
		SHT2 RQ 2
		SH2E B 2
		SH2E C 1
		SH2E I 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/sawedopen")
		SHT2 PO 1
		S2SR AB 1
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SSGShellCasing",25,-2,25,Random(2,4),Random(-3,-6),Random(3,6),0)
		S2SR C 4
		S2SR DEFG 2
		SHT2 L 2 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/shellslide")
		TNT1 A 0
		SHT2 M 2
		SHT2 N 2
		SHT2 OP 1
		SH2E I 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/sawedclose")
		SH2E C 1
		SH2E B 2
		SHT2 QR 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("SSGZombieToken", 1)
		Goto Ready
	}
}

Actor QuadShotgunZombieWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	States
	{
	Ready:
		QSGN A 1 A_WeaponReady
		Goto Ready
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("QSGZombieToken", 2, "Reload")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("QSGZombieToken", 1, "AltFire")
	QuadFire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgfire")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
		TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(10,5,0,1,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("QSGZombieToken", 2)
		TNT1 AAAAAAAAAAAA 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,Random(6,-6))
		QS4F A 2 Bright A_FireBullets(15.4,10.6,24,Random(1,4)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
		QS4F B 3 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		QSGN CFG 1
		QSGN H 2
		QSER A 3
		QSER B 6
		QSGN GFEDC 2
		Goto ReloadFourShellsInstant
	AltFire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("weapons/qsgdoublefire")
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light1
		TNT1 A 0 Radius_Quake(3,3,0,1,0)
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("QSGZombieToken",2,"Reload")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("QSGZombieToken",1,"FireLower")
	FireUpper:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("QSGZombieToken", 1)
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,Random(6,-6))
		QSGF A 2 Bright A_FireBullets(13.8,9.6,10,Random(1,4)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
		QSGF B 3 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		QREC ABCDE 1
		QSGN A 1
		Goto Ready
	FireLower:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GiveInventory("QSGZombieToken", 1)
		TNT1 AAAAAA 0 A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer2",Random(6,-6),0,0,Random(6,-6))
		QSGF C 2 Bright A_FireBullets(13.8,9.6,10,Random(1,4)*3,"MonsterModdedBulletPuff")
		QSGF D 2 Bright A_Light2
		TNT1 A 0 A_Light0
		QREC ABCDE 1
		QSGN A 1
		Goto Reload
	Reload:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("QSGZombieToken",2,"ReloadFourShells")
	ReloadTwoShells:
		QSGN SRQ 2
		QSGN P 1
		QSEX A 1
		QSEX B 1
		TNT1 AA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SSGShellCasing",25,-2,25,Random(2,4),Random(-3,-6),Random(3,6),0)
		QSEX C 1
		QSGR I 12 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgopen")
		QSGR JK 1
		QSGR LM 2
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0
		QSGR N 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgshellslide")
		QSGR O 3
		QSGR P 2
		QSGR Q 1
		QSGN MNO 1
		QSGN P 1 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgclose")
		QSGN QRS 2
		QSGN A 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_TakeInventory("QSGZombieToken", 1)
		Goto Ready
	ReloadFourShells:
		QSGN S 2
	ReloadFourShellsInstant:
		QSGN RQ 2
		QSGN PJ 1
		QSGN K 1
		TNT1 AAAA 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SSGShellCasing",25,-2,25,Random(2,4),Random(-3,-6),Random(3,6),0)
		QSGN L 1
		QSGR A 12 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgopen")
		QSGR B 1
		QSGR CD 2
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0
		QSGR E 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgshellslide")
		QSGR F 3
		QSGR G 2
		QSGR H 1
		QSGR I 8
		QSGR JK 1
		QSGR LM 2
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0
		QSGR N 3 A_PlayWeaponSound("weapons/qsgshellslide")
		QSGR O 3
		QSGR P 2
		QSGR Q 1

	States
	{
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 AA 5
		TNT1 A 4 A_CustomPunch(4)
		TNT1 A 5
		Goto Ready
	AltFire:
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0 A_ReFire
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("cyberfiend/melee")
		TNT1 A 0 ThrustThingZ(0,20,0,1)
		TNT1 A 2 A_Recoil(-24)
		TNT1 A 3 A_FireCustomMissile("PinkyLunge")
		TNT1 A 6
		TNT1 A 2 A_ScaleVelocity(0.2)
		TNT1 A 1 A_ScaleVelocity(0)
		Goto Ready
	}
}


Actor PossessedMagmaFiend : PossessedBullFiend
{
	Player.MorphWeapon "MagmaFiendWeapon"
	Player.StartItem "Attack1"

	Health 250
	PainChance 80
	Speed 0.525 //12
	Scale 1.1
	MaxTargetRange 750
	SeeSound "magma/sight"
	PainSound "monster/psopain"
	DeathSound "magma/death"
	ActiveSound "magma/active"
	AttackSound "magma/attack"
	DropItem "LifeEssence" 105
	DropItem "ArmorBonusMax" 105
	Obituary "%o was massacred by a Magma Fiend."
	HitObituary "%o was gnawed on by a Magma Fiend."
	States
	{
	Spawn:
		SAR3 A 12
		SAI3 A 12
		Loop
	See:
		SAR3 AABB 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("HeavyFleshStep",0,0,0,0)
		SAR3 CCDD 2
		TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("HeavyFleshStep",0,0,0,0)
		Loop
	Missile:
		Goto Spawn
	Melee:
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Attack1", 1, "Fireball")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Attack2", 1, "Lunge")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Attack3", 1, "FlameBreath")
		Goto Spawn
	Fireball:
		SAR3 E 7 
		SAR3 F 6 Bright
		SAR3 E 5 
		Goto Spawn
	Lunge:
		SAR3 F 2 
		SAR3 F 3 
		SAR3 G 6 
		SAR3 G 2 
		SAR3 G 1 
		Goto Spawn
	FlameBreath:
		SAR3 F 5 
		TNT1 A 0
		TNT1 A 0
		SAR3 FFF 2 Bright
		TNT1 A 0
		SAR3 FFF 2 Bright
		TNT1 A 0
		SAR3 FFF 2 Bright
		TNT1 A 0
		SAR3 FFF 2 Bright
		SAR3 E 5 
		Goto Spawn
	}
}

Actor MagmaFiendWeapon : PossessedWeapon
{
	+WEAPON.NOAUTOFIRE

	States
	{
	Fire:
		TNT1 A 0 A_GunFlash
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Attack1", 1, "Fireball")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Attack2", 1, "Lunge")
		TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("Attack3", 1, "FireBreath")
		Goto Ready
	AltFire:
		TNT1 A 0 ACS_ExecuteAlways(mop_magmafiend, 0)
		Goto Ready
	Fireball:
		TNT1 A 7
		TNT1 A 6 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MagmaBall")
		TNT1 A 5
		TNT1 A 0 A_ReFire
		Goto Ready
	Lunge:
		TNT1 A 1
		TNT1 A 0 A_ReFire
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("magma/attack")
		TNT1 A 0 ThrustThingZ(0,20,0,1)
		TNT1 A 2 A_Recoil(-24)
		TNT1 A 3 A_FireCustomMissile("PinkyLunge")
		TNT1 A 6
		TNT1 A 2 A_ScaleVelocity(0.2)
		TNT1 A 1 A_ScaleVelocity(0)
		Goto Ready
	FireBreath:
		TNT1 A 5
		TNT1 A 0 A_PlaySound("magma/firebreath")
		TNT1 AAA 2 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MagmaBreath", Random(6,-6))
		TNT1 AAA 2 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MagmaBreath", Random(6,-6))
		TNT1 AAA 2 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MagmaBreath", Random(6,-6))
		TNT1 AAA 2 Bright A_FireCustomMissile("MagmaBreath", Random(6,-6))
		TNT1 A 15 // +10
		TNT1 A 0 A_ReFire
		Goto Ready
	}
}

		DPNK F 3 Bright

	   	DPNK B 6

		TNT1 A 0 //A_ChangeFlag(SLIDESONWALLS,0)	   
	   	DPNK B 1 //A_ScaleVelocity(0)
		Goto Spawn
	}
}

Actor PossessedHitlerNoSuit : PossessedMonster
{
	Player.MorphWeapon "HitlerNoSuitWeapon"

	Health 1000
	Radius 20
	Height 56
	Speed 0.21875 //5
	Scale 1.2
	PainChance 20
	Mass 1000
	MONSTER
	+FLOORCLIP
	+MISSILEEVENMORE
	+QUICKTORETALIATE
	+NOTARGET
	+LOOKALLAROUND
	DropItem "BulletBox" 256 50
	DropItem "PortableMedkit" 200
	DropItem "ArmorPlate" 200
	DropItem "HandGrenadeAmmo" 200 1
	DropItem "MineAmmo" 200 1
	DropItem "AmmoPack" 150
	DropItem "ExtraArmor" 256 1
	SeeSound "hitler/hahahaha"
	DeathSound "hitler/death1"
	PainSound "monsters/nazipain"
	AttackSound "Null"
	Obituary "%o was executed by the Nazi leader, Adolf Hitler."
	States
	{
	Spawn:
        HTLR A 10 
        Loop
	See:
    	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)
    	HTLR AAAAAABBBBBB 1 
    	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItem("FootStep",0,0,0,0)		
    	HTLR CCCCCCDDDDDD 1 
	    Loop
	Missile:
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer",Random(6,-6),0,0,Random(6,-6))
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 10, 20, 40, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(80, 90), 128)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 10, -20, 40, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_FireBullets(22.5, 0, -1, random(1,5)*3, "MonsterModdedBulletPuff", FBF_NORANDOM)
        HTLR F 3 Bright //A_PlaySoundEx("hitler/fire","Weapon")
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_FireCustomMissile("MonsterTracer",Random(6,-6),0,0,Random(6,-6))
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 10, 20, 40, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(80, 90), 128)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_SpawnItemEx("RifleCasing", 10, -20, 40, Random(2, 6), 0, Random(1, 3), Random(-80, -90), 128)
		TNT1 A 0 Bright //A_FireBullets(22.5, 0, -1, random(1,5)*3, "MonsterModdedBulletPuff", FBF_NORANDOM)		
        HTLR G 3 Bright //A_PlaySoundEx("hitler/fire","Weapon")
		HTLR G 5 Bright
        Goto Spawn
    }
}
